<font size="4">\n[img[master 1]]\n\nYou find master Xi sitting in the school garden at night. You are about to introduce yourself when he turns and says, " You must be the new student. I am master Xi, it is my responsibility to help students understand Tao (the Way).To begin your studies on this subject you must contemplate these words of the great master Confucius:\n\n"What Heaven gives us is called nature. Living in harmony with nature is called the Way. Learning the Way is called 'education.'"\n\nWould you like to see a painting that will help you understand these words better?\n\n[[Yes, I would like to see the painting|Painting of a poet on a mountain]]\n[[Go back to the courtyard]]\n</font>

<font size="4">\n<<loopsound "chinese_music.mp3">>\n[img[country home announcement]]\n\nIt is early morning when an official Ming messenger and two guards approach your family's farmhouse on horseback. The messenger disinterestedly calls to your family, "The time to recruit students for civil service is here. If anyone wishes to enter their county school they must be nominated by the county scholar. You can find the county scholar in his office in town."\n\nHis message given, the group trots off. You consider for a moment and decide that you definitely want to become an imperial scholar.\n\n[[Go and speak with the county scholar|County Scholar]]\n</font>

<font size="4">\n[img[poet on mountain]]\n\nMaster Xi unrolls a piece of paper and indicates for you to take a closer look. He describes the painting, "The man is a poet ascending a mountain. Below, in the trees, you can see his home. The artist of this painting uses the poet as a model for how we must live ."\n\nMaster Xi allows the noises of the night to surround you while you observe the painting. Finally he asks, "What word describes how the poet is living, is it apathy, domination, or harmony?\n\n<<textinput $harmony [[Submit|Harmony]]>>\n</font>

<font size="4">\n[img[...]]\nYou arrive home and see your mother holding a small bundle of bandages. As you approach you can see the anger in her eyes. “How dare you leave this house,” she yells. “After all that we have invested in your future you decide to dishonor us by disappearing.” Holding the bandages out towards you she continues, “ You will put your foot bindings back on immediately and return to your studies.”\n\n[[Go inside to bind your feet|Bind Feet 1]]\n[[Run away into the nearby woods|Run away]]\n</font>
<font size="4">\n[img[county examiner]]\nThe official in green robes greets you, "Welcome to the county school, I am the county examiner. Here at this school we will prepare you for the Ming licensing exam, which you can take any time you feel ready. When you pass this exam you will receive the title Xiucai (flowering talent). This title will grant you admission to the provincial school located in town. However, before you attempt the exam, you should study with the master scholars that we have here. You may move about the school grounds and study at your own pace. Come back to me when you are ready for the exam."\n\n[[Find Master Xi to begin your studies on harmony|Master Xi]] \n[[Find Master Yangming to begin your studies on leadership|Master Yangming]] \n[[Take the exam without studying|Take the licensing exam]]\n</font>

Before you can say anything he continues, "I will attempt to teach you the true path of leadership. To gegin your education on this subject we must heed the words of the great master Confucius." I know your father." Holding up a small bag of coins he countinues, "He gave me twenty good reasons to nominate you for school. I will send word ahead to the school masters about your admission. <font size="4">\n[img[master2 closeup]]\n\nMaster Yangming pauses for a moment and then begins the story.\n\n//Long ago there was an emperor of China who had grown old and he wished to find a wise and worthy person to be emperor when he was gone. \n\nThe old emperor's advisors told him of a boy named Shun who lived in the mountains. The advisors told the emperor that Shun's father and mother were cruel to him and that his brother was arrogant and lazy. Even in such a terrible family, Shun was a loyal son. He can always be seen working on his family's farm without a grudge, even though his family does not help.\n\nThe old emperor was so inspired by Shun's filial piety that he immidiately began training the boy to be emperor. When he decided that Shun was ready, the old emperor gave the throne to Shun and all of China enjoyed peace and happiness.//\n\nAfter finishing the story the master asks, "What quality did the boy possess that made him worthy to be emperor?"\n\n<<textinput $filial_piety [[Submit|Filial Piety]]>>\n</font>
